3/14/20, 08:42 - Ithala: By :- Dr Sunil Karkhanis, Lung Surgeon,  
ex KEM Hospital, Mumbai.


My nephew, who is also a lung specialist now, graduated with a master's degree, and works in *Shenzhen Hospital, China.*  He is being transferred to study *Wuhan pneumonia virus.*  He just called me and told me to tell all of my friends *NOT TO WORRY MUCH ABOUT CORONA VIRUS* : 
If you have a runny nose and sputum when you have a cold, you cannot be a patient of coronavirus pneumonia, because *coronavirus pneumonia is a dry cough without runny nose*. This is the simplest way to identify.

Please tell your friends that if you know more about medical knowledge about this virus, you will have more *awareness of identification and prevention.* 

 This time, the *Wuhan virus is not heat-resistant and will be killed at a temperature of 30-35 degrees*.

 Therefore, *drink more hot water.* You can tell your friends and relatives to drink more hot water to prevent it. *Go under the  Sun for a long time*. It has been cold season recently, and *drinking hot water is also very comfortable. It is not a cure but is a good prevention for the body. Drinking warm water is effective for mostly all viruses*. Try not to drink ice. remember that.

Doctor's advice about coronavirus:

1. It is *pretty large in size* (cell is about *400-500nm diameter*), so *any normal mask (not just the  N95 feature) should be able to filter it out*. However, when someone who's infected sneezes in front of you, it will take a great 3 meters (about 10 feet) before it drops to the ground and is *no longer airborne*. 

2. When the virus drops *on metal surface, it will live for at least 12 hours.* 
So remember if you come in contact with any metal surface, *wash your hands with soap thoroughly. Don't depend on the sanitizers.* 

3. The virus can remain active *on fabric for 6-12 hours*. 
Normal *laundry detergent should kill the virus*. 
For winter clothing that does not require daily washing, you can *put it out under the sun for 4 hours to kill the virus.* 


About the *symptoms of the pneumonia caused by Coronavirus*:

1. It will *first infect the throat, so the throat will have the dry sore throat feeling which will last for 3 to 4 days*

2. Then the virus will blend into the nasal fluid and drips into the trachea and *enter the lungs, causing pneumonia*. This process will *take 5 to 6 days*.    

3. With pneumonia, comes *high fever and difficulty in breathing*. The *nasal congestion* is not like the normal kind. You will feel like *you are drowning in water. It's important to seek immediate medical attention* if you feel like this. 

About *prevention*:

1. The most common way of getting infected is *by touching things in public*, so *you must wash your hands frequently*. The virus can only live on your hands for *5-10 minutes*, but a lot of damage can happen in those 5-10 mins (you may rub your eyes or pick your nose unwittingly).

2. Aside from washing your hands frequently, *you can gargle with Betadine Sore Throat Gargle* to eliminate or minimize the germs *while they are still in your throat (before dripping down to your lungs).* 

Folks, *take extra care and drink plenty of water.*

© Dr Sunil Karkhanis, Lung Surgeon,  
ex KEM Hospital, Mumbai.

Greetings !

IQAC,  Placement Cell,  Department of UG,  PG Studies & Research in Mathematics of Government Science College Autonomous Bengaluru 

in association with

 UJWALA Academy Bengaluru

 Organizing

10 Days National Level
 e - Quiz & e -  Certificate Course

on Mental Ability for Competitive Examinations 

MATHKNACK

From 11/07/2020 to 20/07/2020

Instructions are as follows 

1) Each day 10 Multiple Choice Questions will be released at 9am and will be sent  to registered candidates through their e mail ids

Each Question carries 2 marks,  
No Negative marks for Wrong answers

2) Time to answer all the 10 questions is 24 hours 

3) It is an Open Book Quiz
 
4)No multiple submissions of answers,  
per candidate only one submission, per day

5)At the end of course,  the candidate will receive 
e - Certificate with Grade to their mail id

6)To procure  Certificate, 
All the 10 days submissions are compulsory 

7)e - Certificate with Grade A for procurement of marks 150 to 200, 

e - Certificate with Grade B for procurement of marks 100 to 148,

Participation Certificate  for others

8) The essential qualification is
 10+2 or PUC

9)The following are the Chapters and Dates

11/07/2020 - problems on Percentage

12/07/2020 - Simple and Compound Interest 

13/07/2020 - Profit,  Loss,  Discount 

14/07/2020 - Average 

15/07/2020 - Time,  Speed,  Distance 

16/07/2020 - Time and Work

17/07/2020 - Ratio and Proportion 

18/07/2020 - Problems on Age

19/07/2020 - Permutations and Combinations

20/07/2020 - Probability 

10)No Registration fee to participate in the Quiz

11) The last date for Registration  is 08/07/2020

12)The Quiz is allowed for registered candidates only 

Interested candidates  can register through the link 

https://forms.gle/WCDnBkRjYxp17fBU7

1/7/22, 00:36 - Bharatheesh Mgm: Anyways, all the very best to each and everyone who have got this interview to attend today. And very majorly, just thought of sharing one thought over here. While being in the interview, all you need to make sure is that YOU'RE CONFIDENT about what you're talking. Your language fluency doesn't matter if you've got confidence in your speech without getting confused about what to say... May seem silly but it's not. So please be confident, make it simple and be determined about what you're doing and what you're wanting. All they need is a confident, non complexed and neat employee. (Not even a master of everything or as we say 'scholar in academics')

There are lots of things which we haven't been guided with or haven't spoke about frankly. And that's just to make sure that we don't start neglecting our scores and studies. We've always been taught that scores, English vocabulary and your decency is all that matters. But right now, the need of the hour for every company is an employee who's neat, simple, confident and passionate (not a hard worker, they need smart worker... And you guys know this one point though)

Just in case, even if you feel like you are not in the range of what's expected for the job, please don't express that doubt. Cause that's noted as a dark spot by your interviewers. So please be confident and keep it simple. 
Wishing you all once again, all the very best❤️🙌🏻

And if you've read this whole thing till here, thanks a lot😄

3/13/22, 21:22 - Osama: *MARCH PAST RULES* 

• Each march past team must have a minimum of *40 participants* and no limit for maximum participants

• The teams are awarded 10 marks for their attendance, 10 for their marching and synchronisation, 10 marks for their discipline and 10 for their dispersal.

• The Stream that comes first is awarded 10 points, second gets 7, third gets 3 and the fourth gets 1.

• The results of the March past will be declared by the judges and the decision of the judges stands final.

• The points of Marchpast winners will be added to the Spectrum.
